&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:44:&quot;Dev Blog: WordCamp US 2017-2018 in Nashville&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:34:&quot;https://wordpress.org/news/?p=4571&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:70:&quot;https://wordpress.org/news/2016/11/wordcamp-us-2017-2018-in-nashville/&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:995:&quot;&lt;p&gt;&lt;img class=&quot;aligncenter&quot; src=&quot;https://i0.wp.com/wpdotorg.files.wordpress.com/2008/07/27492741871_c6fcebcad3_k-e1479248587522.jpg?resize=632%2C253&amp;ssl=1&quot; /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The title says it all. We had some great applications for cities to host &lt;a href=&quot;http://us.wordcamp.org/&quot;&gt;WordCamp US&lt;/a&gt; after we finish up in Philadelphia this year, and the city chosen for 2017-2018 is &lt;strong&gt;Nashville, Tennessee&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Based on the other great applications we got I&amp;#8217;m also excited about the pipeline of communities that could host it in future years as WordCamp US travels across the United States and gives us an opportunity to learn and love a new city, as we have with Philadelphia.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;By the way, if you haven&amp;#8217;t yet, now is a great time to &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpressdotorg.polldaddy.com/s/wordpress-2016-survey&quot;&gt;take the Annual WordPress Survey&lt;/a&gt; and ask your friends to as well.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://www.flickr.com/photos/143951935@N07/27492741871&quot;&gt;Photo Credit&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Tue, 15 Nov 2016 23:24:17 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:14:&quot;Matt Mullenweg&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:24;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:90:&quot;WPTavern: Upvato Backup Service Confirms Files Are Lost, Plans to Relaunch on New Provider&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:29:&quot;https://wptavern.com/?p=63862&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:100:&quot;https://wptavern.com/upvato-backup-service-confirms-files-are-lost-plans-to-relaunch-on-new-provider&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:4274:&quot;&lt;p&gt;Upvato creator Freddy Lundekvam has confirmed that all user files entrusted to the service have been permanently lost, as his previous storage provider is unable to recover them. After receiving a series of emails from the provider reminding him that payment was due, the provider terminated his account seven days after the invoice was overdue.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Lundekvam said ordinarily he would expect his sites and servers to go offline in response to an unpaid invoice but this particular provider, which he would not identify, simply terminated his account.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;I contacted the provider in good faith, knowing that any decent provider has complete backups of everything they terminate for X time after they terminate it,&amp;#8221; Lundekvam said. &amp;#8220;Apparently, with this &amp;#8216;crappy&amp;#8217; company, terminated means literally terminated. All decent backup providers have backups of their backups, and any provider with such a setup knows very well that terminating the backups at the same time as you terminate the original files is a HUGE mistake, after all, you have those backups in place just in case something is terminated wrongly or the system corrupts something. We can simply conclude with the fact that this provider didn&amp;#8217;t do backups of their users&amp;#8217; data and therefore would never be able to recover anything they have lost.&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Although Lundekvam mentioned Amazon Glacier in a &lt;a href=&quot;https://wptavern.com/upvato-backup-service-terminated-by-storage-provider-files-may-not-be-recoverable&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;previous interview&lt;/a&gt; as an example of how cheap storage space is, he confirmed that Amazon was not the provider in question here. &amp;#8220;Amazon was quickly ironed out in the launch phase due to the heavy adjustments it needed to make it work exactly the way we wanted it to,&amp;#8221; he said.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Lundekvam said he sincerely believed this backup provider was reliable and was disappointed to find out otherwise after trusting users&amp;#8217; data with the company. Despite the misfortune and embarrassment of the current situation, he is determined to relaunch Upvato with a new provider that offers redundant backups.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;Upvato to Relaunch with Improved Version that Allows Users to Define Backup Destination&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Lundekvam said the new version will be launched &amp;#8220;as soon as possible.&amp;#8221; His team is considering firing up the current (old) version and then migrating as originally planned instead of relaunching with the new version. The improvements include a better backup algorithm and new functionality.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;The very new version will allow the user to define their own destination / choice of backup location, whether that be on Upvato&amp;#8217;s servers, their own FTP / SFTP server, Dropbox, Amazon, and other providers we&amp;#8217;re looking into implementing,&amp;#8221; Lundekvam said. &amp;#8220;This would make Upvato function as a mere gateway that detects and keeps your backups in sync at your favorite destination, while at the same time presenting the same awesome visual experience on the website to display the sales ad associated with the item.&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Lundekvam remains committed to keeping the core service free indefinitely and may add commercial upgrades if costs exceed what he is able to contribute on his own.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;As long as I am able to sustain Upvato on my own, then it will remain ad-free and completely free to use,&amp;#8221; he said. &amp;#8220;But of course there are plans to monetize the website if we at some point need help keeping the lights on. That might be ad-generated revenue, or a premium service for premium functionality. But regardless of what we do then, the core functionality of Upvato &amp;#8211; backing up your Envato files &amp;#8211; will always remain free to use.&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;In response to commenters who suspected the service of fraud and users who may be wary of continuing with the service, Lundekvam said, &amp;#8220;Upvato is not a fraud in any way. It&amp;#8217;s really entirely up to the user if they want to give us a second chance or not. We are a completely free service that intends to do the very best we can do make sure that we stay a reliable, good way to store and backup your Envato files.&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div id=&quot;epoch-width-sniffer&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Tue, 15 Nov 2016 22:48:53 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;Sarah Gooding&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:25;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:85:&quot;WPTavern: WordPress 4.7 Improves Accessibility by Removing Alternative Text Fallbacks&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:29:&quot;https://wptavern.com/?p=63819&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:96:&quot;https://wptavern.com/wordpress-4-7-improves-accessibility-by-removing-alternative-text-fallbacks&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:1252:&quot;&lt;p&gt;When images are uploaded in WordPress 4.6.1 that have an empty alt text value, WordPress tries to generate one based on the caption text or the image title. If the image title is non descriptive as is common with photos uploaded from digital cameras, the alt text can be meaningless.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;In WordPress 4.7, the caption text and the image title fallbacks have been removed. The fallbacks were originally introduced to ensure every image included alternative text. Over time however, this practice has proven to be a poor user experience for people who use screen readers.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Since the fallbacks are removed, users will need to explicitly set a value for the alt text field. &lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/2016/11/11/improving-accessibility-of-image-alternative-text-in-4-7/&quot;&gt;According to Joe McGill&lt;/a&gt;, the change will not affect content already published but will be the expected behavior in WordPress 4.7 and beyond.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;If you&amp;#8217;re not sure what text to use to describe an image, check &lt;a href=&quot;http://webaim.org/techniques/alttext/#basics&quot;&gt;out this article &lt;/a&gt;on Webaim. It explains when alt text should be displayed and provides useful tips on how to describe an image.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div id=&quot;epoch-width-sniffer&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Tue, 15 Nov 2016 18:51:23 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;Jeff Chandler&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:26;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:64:&quot;WPTavern: Wedding Bride: A Free One-Page WordPress Wedding Theme&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:29:&quot;https://wptavern.com/?p=60375&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:74:&quot;https://wptavern.com/wedding-bride-a-free-one-page-wordpress-wedding-theme&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:2864:&quot;&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/themes/wedding-bride/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Wedding Bride&lt;/a&gt; is a new theme from Alex Itsios, co-founder of &lt;a href=&quot;https://ketchupthemes.com/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Ketchup Themes&lt;/a&gt;. The Cyprus-based theme company has &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/themes/author/alexitsios/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;16 themes on WordPress.org&lt;/a&gt;. Wedding themes are a relatively small niche in the directory with fewer than 20 listings. This new arrival stands out from the pack with its bold colors and customizability.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Many WordPress wedding themes in the official directory seem like a wedding site forced into a blog-oriented design, with lingering post meta in areas where it serves no purpose. This particular niche is where a focused, one-page design really shines. Wedding Bride features event-specific front page sections for the couple to share their story but also allows for (optional) extra pages and a blog.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://i2.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/wedding-bride-screenshot.png?ssl=1&quot;&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;https://i2.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/wedding-bride-screenshot.png?resize=880%2C660&amp;ssl=1&quot; alt=&quot;wedding-bride-screenshot&quot; class=&quot;aligncenter size-full wp-image-60380&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;All of the theme&amp;#8217;s options can be found in the Customizer where users can upload a header image, personalize the header overlay, and add various content sections &amp;#8211; all of which are optional. It also includes an option to make the navigation menu sticky or have it scroll with the page (default).&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://i0.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/wedding-bride-theme-1.png?ssl=1&quot;&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;https://i0.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/wedding-bride-theme-1.png?resize=1025%2C405&amp;ssl=1&quot; alt=&quot;wedding-bride-theme&quot; class=&quot;aligncenter size-full wp-image-63806&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Wedding Bride users can customize the background color and/or image. Unfortunately, the theme does not include a color picker to customize the pink accent color, but this can be changed with a little CSS. Blog pages include a sidebar and it supports four widget areas in the footer. The contact form section was created for use with &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/plugins/contact-form-7/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Contact Form 7&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Check out the &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.platotheme.com/wedding-version/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;live demo&lt;/a&gt; to see the theme in action. &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/themes/wedding-bride/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Wedding Bride&lt;/a&gt; is Alex Itsios&amp;#8217; 16th theme on WordPress.org and his first foray into the wedding niche. If you&amp;#8217;re looking for a theme that allows you to quickly create a wedding website with all the essential details on one page, you can download it for free from WordPress.org via your admin themes browser.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div id=&quot;epoch-width-sniffer&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Tue, 15 Nov 2016 06:28:50 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;Sarah Gooding&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:27;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:65:&quot;WPTavern: WP eCommerce 3.11.4 Patches SQL Injection Vulnerability&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:29:&quot;https://wptavern.com/?p=63743&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:76:&quot;https://wptavern.com/wp-ecommerce-3-11-4-patches-sql-injection-vulnerability&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:1138:&quot;&lt;p&gt;Over the weekend, the WP eCommerce team released version 3.11.4 of its &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/plugins/wp-e-commerce/&quot;&gt;e-commerce plugin&lt;/a&gt;. The update patches an SQL injection vulnerability that was responsibly disclosed by Mika Epstein, a member of the WordPress.org plugin review team.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://wpecommerce.org/news/wp-ecommerce-3-11-4-security-update/&quot;&gt;According to Justin Sainton&lt;/a&gt;, lead developer of WP eCommerce, the team was notified of the vulnerability on November 11th and patched within an hour. The update was available on WordPress.org the following day.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;This vulnerability only affects users who use eWay as their payment gateway, have Gold Cart activated, and are using the as-of-yet-unreleased Theme Engine 2.0,&amp;#8221; Sainton said.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;We believe the number of users affected is likely close to zero, due to these conditions.&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Users are highly encouraged to update as soon as possible. Created in 2006, WP eCommerce is one of the oldest plugins in the directory and is actively installed on more than 40K sites.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div id=&quot;epoch-width-sniffer&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Tue, 15 Nov 2016 00:34:17 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;Jeff Chandler&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:28;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:92:&quot;WPTavern: Upvato Backup Service Terminated by Storage Provider, Files May Not be Recoverable&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:29:&quot;https://wptavern.com/?p=63352&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:102:&quot;https://wptavern.com/upvato-backup-service-terminated-by-storage-provider-files-may-not-be-recoverable&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:5185:&quot;&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://i0.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/upvato-featured.png?ssl=1&quot;&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;https://i0.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/upvato-featured.png?resize=1025%2C471&amp;ssl=1&quot; alt=&quot;upvato-featured&quot; class=&quot;aligncenter size-full wp-image-50622&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://www.upvato.com/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upvato&lt;/a&gt;, the service that specializes in backing up Envato Market files, has shut down without warning. Freddy Lundekvam, a full time programmer and frequent user of Envato products, created the service after losing 10 files to Envato&amp;#8217;s policy of reserving the right to take down and remove any file at its or the author&amp;#8217;s sole discretion. Losing files is a &lt;a href=&quot;https://forums.envato.com/t/half-of-my-items-removed/27143/3&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;common frustration among Envato users&lt;/a&gt;, as the company cannot guarantee the ongoing availability of products due to situations like copyright complaints and technical issues.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Upvato made it easy for users to automatically backup their purchases, cataloguing them with screenshots, descriptions, titles, and author information. The service offered unlimited backups and Lundekvam encouraged users to connect their Envato accounts to keep their files safe. A few weeks ago, Upvato users started to suspect that the service was shutting down.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote class=&quot;twitter-tweet&quot;&gt;&lt;p lang=&quot;en&quot; dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;Anyone using &lt;a href=&quot;https://twitter.com/hashtag/Upvato?src=hash&quot;&gt;#Upvato&lt;/a&gt; for their themes etc from &lt;a href=&quot;https://twitter.com/envato&quot;&gt;@envato&lt;/a&gt; &amp;#8211; I think you have just been duped!&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;mdash; Andrew Wilkinson (@parysnet) &lt;a href=&quot;https://twitter.com/parysnet/status/793135773998514176&quot;&gt;October 31, 2016&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote class=&quot;twitter-tweet&quot;&gt;&lt;p lang=&quot;en&quot; dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;What happened to &lt;a href=&quot;https://twitter.com/hashtag/upvato?src=hash&quot;&gt;#upvato&lt;/a&gt;? Looks like it died silently and nobody noticed. Zero commentary from the usual webdev pundits.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;mdash; sunil (@sunilwilliams) &lt;a href=&quot;https://twitter.com/sunilwilliams/status/791535374971523072&quot;&gt;October 27, 2016&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;I&amp;#8217;m beginning to think this was not all above board,&amp;#8221; one WP Tavern commenter &lt;a href=&quot;https://wptavern.com/new-upvato-service-offers-free-backups-for-envato-market-products#comment-202262&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;said&lt;/a&gt; after discovering that the site disappeared. &amp;#8220;[Upvato] seamlessly copied all my themes to their server and then shut down with no warning!&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Lundekvam, whose website can no longer be reached, replied to my first inquiry. After experiencing problems with Upvato&amp;#8217;s provider, he is not hopeful that he can recover the files.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;Our provider&amp;#8217;s automated systems terminated everything related to Upvato,&amp;#8221; Lundekvam said. &amp;#8220;I am so frustrated and upset that you won&amp;#8217;t believe it, but I am doing what I can do recover the files and or get a backup up and running. But it seems like the provider isn&amp;#8217;t and wasn&amp;#8217;t really a reliable backup provider at all, and as it is right now, it looks really dark for a possible chance to recover the files.&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Lundekvam would not specify who his provider was, but had referenced Amazon Glacier in a &lt;a href=&quot;https://wptavern.com/new-upvato-service-offers-free-backups-for-envato-market-products&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;previous interview&lt;/a&gt; as an example of cheap storage space at a mere $7/month.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;Such things shouldn&amp;#8217;t happen with a backup provider like Upvato, and I am extremely surprised that it happened with our backup provider, causing it to affect Upvato,&amp;#8221; he said. He also confirmed that he does not plan to shut the service down permanently.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;If I am unable to recover the backup and files, then no, I am not shutting down,&amp;#8221; Lundekvam said.&amp;#8221; I would, and have to, install Upvato with a new provider and start over. Please rest assured that Upvato is coming back up. Regarding the concerned users, I am deeply sorry for the downtime and, possibly, loss of Envato files. It hurts that it happened, as this is in no way how I want Upvato to be seen or represented.&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Lundekvam would not respond to subsequent inquiries. Upvato has had ample time to share this news via other outlets but the service did not have a Twitter account and its website has vanished, leaving users without any information. Lundekvam had said in previous interviews that he did not have plans to monetize Upvato in the immediate future. His motivation was to &amp;#8220;make something cool and useful that people might want and need.&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Unfortunately, since he treated Upvato as a side project and did not have further backups in place, an unexpected problem with his provider has wiped out the files users trusted with the service. In an ironic twist, the service has inadvertantly replicated the exact situation that users hoped to avoid with Envato. Lundekvam has not responded to further inquiries on the status of the recovery process, but we will update when any new information is available.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div id=&quot;epoch-width-sniffer&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Mon, 14 Nov 2016 21:01:57 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;Sarah Gooding&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:29;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:34:&quot;Matt: Flying Lotus, Never Catch Me&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:22:&quot;https://ma.tt/?p=46928&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:50:&quot;https://ma.tt/2016/11/flying-lotus-never-catch-me/&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:357:&quot;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Music videos are themselves an art form, and it&amp;#8217;s always interesting to me how an artist chooses to transform the interpretation of their song with the video. I&amp;#8217;ve listened to this song since it came out but haven&amp;#8217;t seen the video until now, and it will definitely make me listen to it differently. Featuring Kendrick Lamar.&lt;/p&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Sun, 13 Nov 2016 18:49:52 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:4:&quot;Matt&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:30;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:58:&quot;WPTavern: New WordPress Plugin Serves Pre-Compressed Emoji&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:29:&quot;https://wptavern.com/?p=63682&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:69:&quot;https://wptavern.com/new-wordpress-plugin-serves-pre-compressed-emoji&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:3475:&quot;&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://i2.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/11/compressed-emoji.png?ssl=1&quot;&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;https://i2.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/11/compressed-emoji.png?resize=627%2C250&amp;ssl=1&quot; alt=&quot;compressed-emoji&quot; class=&quot;aligncenter size-full wp-image-63714&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;WordPress emoji are served from s.w.org, but they are not compressed. This impacts the SVG loading time, depending on how many emoji you are using, and can even throw warnings on Google&amp;#8217;s &lt;a href=&quot;https://developers.google.com/speed/pagespeed/insights/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;PageSpeed Insights&lt;/a&gt; tool. Turkey-based WordPress developer &lt;a href=&quot;https://profiles.wordpress.org/m_uysl/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Mustafa Uysal&lt;/a&gt; has just released &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/plugins/compressed-emoji/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Compressed Emoji&lt;/a&gt;, a plugin that makes use of the &lt;a href=&quot;https://developer.wordpress.org/reference/hooks/emoji_svg_url/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;emoji_svg_url&lt;/a&gt; filter introduced in 4.6. This filter allows developers to change the URL for where emoji SVG images are hosted.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;When the plugin is activated, the compression offers savings in the range of 3kb ~ 1.3kb (roughly %60) per emoji.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://i1.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/11/emoji-compressed-comparison.png?ssl=1&quot;&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;https://i1.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/11/emoji-compressed-comparison.png?resize=1025%2C511&amp;ssl=1&quot; alt=&quot;emoji-compressed-comparison&quot; class=&quot;aligncenter size-full wp-image-63717&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Uysal said he hopes WordPress.org will consider compressing emoji in the future, especially since approximately 10% of the web is using WordPress 4.6. Compressing emoji is a small way to speed up a sizeable chunk of the web. A &lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/ticket/37374&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;ticket&lt;/a&gt; was created on Trac four months ago, requesting cache headers for emoji files and compression. According to Gary Pendergast, the change is something that can be made outside of the WordPress core development cycle, so he closed the ticket and &lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/systems/2016/07/20/there-are-no-cache-instructions/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;passed the suggestion on to the Systems team&lt;/a&gt;. Cache headers were added by the team, but compression was not implemented in that update.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;The current plan is to move everything to a new CDN,&amp;#8221; Gary Pendergast reported after chatting with the Systems team. &amp;#8220;The current CDN is a bit outdated &amp;#8211; they don’t support HTTP/2, for example. They need to do some more testing, but it’s high on the todo list.&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;In the meantime, users who want compressed emoji can use Uysal&amp;#8217;s plugin. It compressed the files using &lt;a href=&quot;https://github.com/svg/svgo&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;SVGO&lt;/a&gt;, an open source Node.js-based tool for optimizing SVG vector graphics files. The tool removes unnecessary things like metadata, comments, hidden elements, and default or non-optimal values from the SVG files without affecting their rendering. Another advantage is it doesn&amp;#8217;t require an internet connection for those who are developing locally.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/plugins/compressed-emoji/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Compressed Emoji&lt;/a&gt; is available in the WordPress plugin directory and is also open for contributions on &lt;a href=&quot;https://github.com/mustafauysal/compressed-emoji&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;GitHub&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div id=&quot;epoch-width-sniffer&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Fri, 11 Nov 2016 23:49:19 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;Sarah Gooding&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:31;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:30:&quot;Dev Blog: WordPress 4.7 Beta 3&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:34:&quot;https://wordpress.org/news/?p=4566&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:56:&quot;https://wordpress.org/news/2016/11/wordpress-4-7-beta-3/&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:3091:&quot;&lt;p&gt;WordPress 4.7 Beta 3 is now available!&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;This software is still in development,&lt;/strong&gt; so we don’t recommend you run it on a production site. Consider setting up a test site just to play with the new version. To test WordPress 4.7, try the &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/plugins/wordpress-beta-tester/&quot;&gt;WordPress Beta Tester&lt;/a&gt; plugin (you’ll want “bleeding edge nightlies”). Or you can &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/wordpress-4.7-beta3.zip&quot;&gt;download the beta here&lt;/a&gt; (zip).&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;For more information on what’s new in 4.7, check out the &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/news/2016/10/wordpress-4-7-beta-1/&quot;&gt;Beta 1&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/news/2016/11/wordpress-4-7-beta-2/&quot;&gt;Beta 2&lt;/a&gt; blog posts, along with &lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/tag/4-7+dev-notes/&quot;&gt;in-depth field guides on make/core&lt;/a&gt;. Some of the changes in Beta 3 include:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;REST API:&lt;/strong&gt; The &lt;code&gt;unfiltered_html&lt;/code&gt; capability is now respected and &lt;code&gt;rest_base&lt;/code&gt; has been added to response objects of &lt;code&gt;wp/v2/taxonomies&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;wp/v2/types&lt;/code&gt;, while &lt;code&gt;get_allowed_query_vars()&lt;/code&gt; and the &lt;code&gt;rest_get_post&lt;/code&gt; filter have been removed.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Roles/Capabilities:&lt;/strong&gt; Added meta-caps for comment, term, and user meta, which are currently only used in the REST API.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;I18N:&lt;/strong&gt; Added the ability to change user&amp;#8217;s locale back to site&amp;#8217;s locale. (&lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/ticket/38632&quot;&gt;#38632&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Custom CSS:&lt;/strong&gt; Renamed the &lt;code&gt;unfiltered_css&lt;/code&gt; meta capability to &lt;code&gt;edit_css&lt;/code&gt; and added revisions support to the &lt;code&gt;custom_css&lt;/code&gt; post type.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Edit shortcuts:&lt;/strong&gt; Theme authors should take a look at &lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/2016/11/10/visible-edit-shortcuts-in-the-customizer-preview/&quot;&gt;the developer guide to the customizer preview&amp;#8217;s visible edit shortcuts&lt;/a&gt; and update their themes to take advantage of them if not already implementing selective refresh.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Various bug fixes:&lt;/strong&gt; We’ve made &lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/log/trunk/src?action=stop_on_copy&amp;mode=stop_on_copy&amp;rev=39200&amp;stop_rev=39143&amp;limit=200&amp;verbose=on&amp;sfp_email=&amp;sfph_mail=&quot;&gt;over 50 changes&lt;/a&gt; in the last week.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Do you speak a language other than English? &lt;a href=&quot;https://translate.wordpress.org/projects/wp/dev&quot;&gt;Help us translate WordPress into more than 100 languages!&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;If you think you’ve found a bug&lt;/strong&gt;, you can post to the &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/support/forum/alphabeta&quot;&gt;Alpha/Beta area&lt;/a&gt; in the support forums. We’d love to hear from you! If you’re comfortable writing a reproducible bug report, &lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/reports/&quot;&gt;file one on WordPress Trac&lt;/a&gt;, where you can also find &lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/tickets/major&quot;&gt;a list of known bugs&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Building the future&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;em&gt;A global community&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;em&gt;Stronger together&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Fri, 11 Nov 2016 03:30:52 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:15:&quot;Helen Hou-Sandi&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:32;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:52:&quot;WPTavern: Andy Baio Relaunches Waxy.org on WordPress&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:29:&quot;https://wptavern.com/?p=63685&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:63:&quot;https://wptavern.com/andy-baio-relaunches-waxy-org-on-wordpress&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:3333:&quot;&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://i0.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/11/waxy.png?ssl=1&quot;&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;https://i0.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/11/waxy.png?resize=1025%2C415&amp;ssl=1&quot; alt=&quot;waxy&quot; class=&quot;aligncenter size-full wp-image-63701&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;After 14 years of blogging with MovableType, Andy Baio has &lt;a href=&quot;http://waxy.org/2016/11/redesigning-waxy-2016-edition/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;relaunched Waxy.org on WordPress&lt;/a&gt;. Baio&amp;#8217;s media and technology blog has been a continual source of original content about life on the internet and how it affects our culture. The migration includes 472 posts and 15,891 entries from his sideblog &lt;a href=&quot;http://waxy.org/category/links/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Waxy Links&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Waxy.org played a small part in WordPress.org&amp;#8217;s early history. In 2005 Baio broke the story about &lt;a href=&quot;http://waxy.org/2005/03/wordpress_websi/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;WordPress quietly hosting search engine spam articles&lt;/a&gt; in order to help cover some of the site&amp;#8217;s expenses. The exposure and subsequent removal of &lt;a href=&quot;http://random.waxy.org/html/google_wordpress.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;the articles&lt;/a&gt; temporarily decimated WordPress.org&amp;#8217;s pagerank but Matt Mullenweg&amp;#8217;s &lt;a href=&quot;https://ma.tt/2005/04/a-response/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;response&lt;/a&gt; to the situation brought more transparency to how the open source project was being funded. Baio interviewed Mullenweg for the piece and considered it his first foray into serious journalism.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;In his post about the site&amp;#8217;s redesign Baio concedes that blogs are &amp;#8220;not really part of the cultural conversation anymore&amp;#8221; but said he thinks there&amp;#8217;s still potential in the medium.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;There a few reasons why I’m sad about the decline of independent blogging, and why I think they’re still worth fighting for,&amp;#8221; Baio said. &amp;#8220;Ultimately, it comes down to two things: ownership and control.&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Baio explained why it&amp;#8217;s important for him to control his own space on the web, as opposed to putting content at the mercy of third-party platforms whose futures are not guaranteed:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;&lt;p&gt;Last week, Twitter announced they’re shutting down Vine. Twitter, itself, may be acquired and changed in some terrible way. It’s not hard to imagine a post-Verizon Yahoo selling off Tumblr. Medium keeps pivoting, trying to find a successful revenue model. There’s no guarantee any of these platforms will be around in their current state in a year, let alone ten years from now.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Here, I control my words. Nobody can shut this site down, run annoying ads on it, or sell it to a phone company. Nobody can tell me what I can or can’t say, and I have complete control over the way it’s displayed. Nobody except me can change the URL structure, breaking 14 years of links to content on the web.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://waxy.org/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Waxy.org&lt;/a&gt; is now responsive and uses a custom theme built using Automattic&amp;#8217;s &lt;a href=&quot;http://components.underscores.me/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Components starter-theme generator&lt;/a&gt;. Baio will continue exploring odd corners of the internet on his blog and plans to share his thoughts about the challenges of navigating the ecosystem of independent publishers.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div id=&quot;epoch-width-sniffer&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Thu, 10 Nov 2016 23:45:20 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;Sarah Gooding&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:33;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:57:&quot;WPTavern: bbPress 2.5.11 Adds WordPress 4.7 Compatibility&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:29:&quot;https://wptavern.com/?p=63694&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:68:&quot;https://wptavern.com/bbpress-2-5-11-adds-wordpress-4-7-compatibility&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:2494:&quot;&lt;p&gt;The bbPress development team has &lt;a href=&quot;https://bbpress.org/blog/2016/11/bbpress-2-5-11-maintenance-release/&quot;&gt;released 2.5.11&lt;/a&gt; to add support &lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/2016/11/07/changed-loading-order-for-current-user-in-4-7/&quot;&gt;for a technical change&lt;/a&gt; in WordPress 4.7. Users are highly encouraged to update to bbPress 2.5.11 &lt;strong&gt;before&lt;/strong&gt; updating to WordPress 4.7. In 4.7, the loading order for the current user in the function stack was changed to accommodate &lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/2016/11/07/user-admin-languages-and-locale-switching-in-4-7/&quot;&gt;user locale switching&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Previously, BuddyPress and bbPress displayed a custom notice when a user was initialized without using WP-&amp;gt;init(). In addition to patching the issue in &lt;a href=&quot;https://buddypress.trac.wordpress.org/ticket/7305&quot;&gt;BuddyPress&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href=&quot;https://bbpress.trac.wordpress.org/ticket/2309&quot;&gt;bbPress&lt;/a&gt;, a new &lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/ticket/23016&quot;&gt;wp_roles_init filter&lt;/a&gt; was added to WordPress that allows plugins to add custom roles when they&amp;#8217;re initialized.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The changes mentioned above are technical in nature so I asked John James Jacoby, lead developer of bbPress, what the update really means. &amp;#8220;bbPress loads its roles on-the-fly, in a similar way to how post-types and taxonomies are registered,&amp;#8221; Jacoby told the Tavern.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;With locales and roles now having a reversed load order, bbPress needed some code changes to work for both WordPress 4.6 and 4.7 without causing any problems for third-party bbPress plugins and non-English installations.&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;This particular improvement has personal historical meaning to Jacoby, &amp;#8220;This change to WordPress core in 4.7 is a long time coming,&amp;#8221; he said.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;It was the very first bug I ever reported in WordPress&amp;#8217; IRC channel back in 2008, when I was working on a large multi-lingual multisite installation. It&amp;#8217;s how I met Peter Westwood and Jen Mylo, and it was their kindness that made it clear that WordPress was the platform for me.&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Jacoby also notes that per-forum moderators, favorites, and subscriptions have been rewritten in bbPress 2.6. During testing, performance enhancements were discovered and submitted to WordPress core and have been implemented across the forums on WordPress.org. Work continues on bbPress 2.6 which is expected to ship in 2017.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div id=&quot;epoch-width-sniffer&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Thu, 10 Nov 2016 22:33:44 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;Jeff Chandler&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:34;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;

WordCamp US live stream tickets will be free this year and development of BuddyPress 2.8 kicks off. We talk about the revamped guidelines for the WordPress plugin directory and how they should help streamline the review process.&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;h2&gt;Plugins Picked By Marcus:&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/plugins/grid-canvas-pinterest/&quot;&gt;Grid Canvas &amp;#8211; Pinterest Image Creator &lt;/a&gt;automatically detects all the images in a post and adds them to a grid layout. It comes with plenty of predefined grid layouts to choose from and there are more coming soon. You can also select the image size that is most optimal for different social networks.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/plugins/disable-password-changed-notifications/&quot;&gt;Disable Password Changed Notifications&lt;/a&gt; by Pippin Williamson disables the notification email sent to site administrators when users change their passwords.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/plugins/wp-private-comment-notes/&quot;&gt;WP Private Comment Notes&lt;/a&gt; allows WordPress admins and or moderators to add and manage private notes for comments. Additionally, each note can be shared with the user who left the original comment.&lt;/p&gt;
