For more information, check out their &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.gravityforms.com/&quot;&gt;website&lt;/a&gt; and thank you to Gravity Forms for being a Post Status partner.&lt;/p&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Mon, 07 Nov 2016 14:38:13 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:14:&quot;Katie Richards&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:44;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:82:&quot;WPTavern: WordPress Plugin Team Publishes Revamped Guidelines for Plugin Directory&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:29:&quot;https://wptavern.com/?p=63410&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:93:&quot;https://wptavern.com/wordpress-plugin-team-publishes-revamped-guidelines-for-plugin-directory&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:3100:&quot;&lt;a href=&quot;https://i0.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/writing.jpg?ssl=1&quot;&gt;&lt;img src=&quot;https://i0.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/writing.jpg?resize=1025%2C472&amp;ssl=1&quot; alt=&quot;photo credit: Green Chameleon&quot; class=&quot;size-full wp-image-51302&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;photo credit: &lt;a href=&quot;https://stocksnap.io/photo/8Y0EDX4VP9&quot;&gt;Green Chameleon&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Two months ago, revised guidelines for the WordPress Plugin Directory were &lt;a href=&quot;https://wptavern.com/wordpress-plugin-team-revamps-guidelines-invites-feedback-on-github&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;opened up on GitHub for public feedback&lt;/a&gt;. This transparent and open process of updating the guidelines resulted in more than a dozen contributors submitting pull requests with improvements to the language and content. The &lt;a href=&quot;https://developer.wordpress.org/plugins/wordpress-org/detailed-plugin-guidelines/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;revamped guidelines&lt;/a&gt; have now replaced the previous ones with language and expectations that are clearer and easier to understand.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;In addition to rewriting the guidelines, we took the time to codify the expectations of developers and cost of not abiding by the guidelines, as well as a reminder that we do remove plugins for security issues,&amp;#8221; plugin team member Mika Epstein said in the &lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/plugins/2016/11/01/revised-guidelines-are-live/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;announcement&lt;/a&gt;. &amp;#8220;We are doing our best to be transparent of what we expect from you and, in return, what you can expect from us.&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;After several incidents this year where unclear guidelines contributed to confusion on issues like &lt;a href=&quot;https://wptavern.com/wordpress-plugin-directory-cracks-down-on-incentivized-reviews-despite-lack-of-official-guideline&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;incentivized reviews&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href=&quot;https://wptavern.com/the-wordpress-plugin-directory-will-no-longer-accept-frameworks&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;developers submitting frameworks&lt;/a&gt;, the plugin team made the jump to update the five-year-old document. Although there are not major changes, some of the guidelines were considerably expanded for clarity. This includes #9: &amp;#8220;The plugin and its developers must not do anything illegal, dishonest, or morally offensive.&amp;#8221; The list was updated with several more examples of infractions that would land under this category.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&amp;#8220;It’s a massive undertaking to re-write guidelines in the public eye in a way that won’t pull the rug out from anyone,&amp;#8221; Epstein said. &amp;#8220;Our goal was to clarify, not totally change, but also to address the needs of an ever changing technology.&amp;#8221;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Because the plugin directory was created to serve the WordPress project and its users, it doesn&amp;#8217;t function like many other popular directories and marketplaces. Clear language and expectations are important, especially with WordPress&amp;#8217; growing international user base. The newly updated guidelines should cut down on incidents where the plugin team has to enforce guidelines that were not explicitly documented.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div id=&quot;epoch-width-sniffer&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Mon, 07 Nov 2016 06:03:59 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;Sarah Gooding&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:45;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:28:&quot;BuddyPress: BuddyPress 2.7.2&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:32:&quot;https://buddypress.org/?p=260750&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:48:&quot;https://buddypress.org/2016/11/buddypress-2-7-2/&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:888:&quot;&lt;p&gt;BuddyPress 2.7.2 is now available. This is a maintenance release and a recommended upgrade for all BuddyPress installations.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;BP 2.7.2 fixes a bug which ignored deprecated code being used in existing installations. For more information, see &lt;a href=&quot;https://buddypress.trac.wordpress.org/query?group=status&amp;milestone=2.7.2&quot;&gt;the 2.7.2 milestone&lt;/a&gt; on &lt;a href=&quot;https://buddypress.trac.wordpress.org/&quot;&gt;BuddyPress Trac&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Update to BuddyPress 2.7.2 today in your WordPress Dashboard, or by &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/plugins/buddypress/&quot;&gt;downloading from the wordpress.org plugin repository&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Questions or comments? Check out &lt;a href=&quot;https://codex.buddypress.org/releases/version-2-7-2/&quot;&gt;2.7.2 changelog&lt;/a&gt;, or stop by &lt;a href=&quot;https://buddypress.org/support/&quot;&gt;our support forums&lt;/a&gt; or &lt;a href=&quot;https://buddypress.trac.wordpress.org/&quot;&gt;Trac&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Sat, 05 Nov 2016 16:30:14 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:8:&quot;@mercime&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:46;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:68:&quot;WPTavern: PressNomics 5 Scheduled for April 6-8, 2017 in Phoenix, AZ&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:29:&quot;https://wptavern.com/?p=63490&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:77:&quot;https://wptavern.com/pressnomics-5-scheduled-for-april-6-8-2017-in-phoenix-az&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:1928:&quot;&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://pressnomics.com/&quot;&gt;PressNomics&lt;/a&gt;, an annual conference devoted to the economics of WordPress &lt;a href=&quot;https://pressnomics.com/2016/11/pressnomics-5-april-6th-8th-2017/&quot;&gt;has announced&lt;/a&gt; that the fifth iteration of the event will take place April 6-8, 2017 at Tempe Mission Palms Hotel, in Phoenix, AZ. The event is organized by Joshua Strebel of &lt;a title=&quot;http://page.ly&quot; href=&quot;http://page.ly&quot;&gt;Pagely&lt;/a&gt;, a managed WordPress hosting company that recently celebrated its &lt;a href=&quot;https://pagely.com/blog/2016/09/managed-wordpress-hosting-7yrs/&quot;&gt;seventh birthday&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;A hallmark of the event is its contributions to charity. Since PressNomics one, the event has raised more than $40K for various charities including, &lt;a href=&quot;http://www.stjude.org&quot;&gt;St. Jude Children&amp;#8217;s Research Hospital&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a href=&quot;http://curesearch.org&quot;&gt;CureSearch.org&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a href=&quot;https://bensbells.org/&quot;&gt;BensBells&lt;/a&gt;, and Big Brothers and Big Sisters.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;In addition to the conference, there will be a social Saturday where attendees can participate in a golf tournament or go on an excursion to explore the Art&amp;#8217;s and Culture of the area. The social activities will be available as a separate purchase of $50 when buying your tickets. To take full advantage of the event, organizers suggest that attendees fly in on Wednesday, April 5th and leave on Sunday, April 9th.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Tickets have yet to go on sale and the speaker lineup is in the process of being finalized. If you want to be one of the first to know when tickets go on sale, you&amp;#8217;re encouraged to sign up to the &lt;a href=&quot;https://pressnomics.com/&quot;&gt;event&amp;#8217;s email list&lt;/a&gt;. For insight into what it&amp;#8217;s like to attend PressNomics, check out my &lt;a href=&quot;https://wptavern.com/envato-stats-tips-for-getting-things-done-and-more-at-pressnomics-3&quot;&gt;review of PressNomics 3 &lt;/a&gt;held in January of 2015.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div id=&quot;epoch-width-sniffer&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Fri, 04 Nov 2016 18:53:29 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;Jeff Chandler&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:47;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:30:&quot;Dev Blog: WordPress 4.7 Beta 2&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:34:&quot;https://wordpress.org/news/?p=4552&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:56:&quot;https://wordpress.org/news/2016/11/wordpress-4-7-beta-2/&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:4195:&quot;&lt;p&gt;WordPress 4.7 Beta 2 is now available!&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;This software is still in development,&lt;/strong&gt; so we don’t recommend you run it on a production site. Consider setting up a test site just to play with the new version. To test WordPress 4.7, try the &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/plugins/wordpress-beta-tester/&quot;&gt;WordPress Beta Tester&lt;/a&gt; plugin (you’ll want “bleeding edge nightlies”). Or you can &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/wordpress-4.7-beta2.zip&quot;&gt;download the beta here&lt;/a&gt; (zip).&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Notable changes since WordPress 4.7 Beta 1:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Twenty Seventeen:&lt;/strong&gt; The theme wasn&amp;#8217;t being installed on upgrades &amp;#8211; sorry about that! Now you should see it if you&amp;#8217;re upgrading an existing site. There are also plenty of fixes, especially for the header and small screen views.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Edit shortcuts:&lt;/strong&gt; These are always visible while editing (hide them on bigger screens by collapsing the controls) and should now work properly in Firefox. (&lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/ticket/27403&quot;&gt;#27403&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/ticket/38532&quot;&gt;#38532&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;REST API endpoints:&lt;/strong&gt; There have been a number of changes over the past week; your attention is requested on the following:
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;The &lt;code&gt;DELETE&lt;/code&gt; response format has changed and may need to be accounted for. (&lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/ticket/38494&quot;&gt;#38494&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Enabled querying by multiple post statuses. (&lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/ticket/38420&quot;&gt;#38420&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Return an error when JSON decoding fails. (&lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/ticket/38547&quot;&gt;#38547&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;More developer notes&lt;/strong&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/2016/10/28/fine-grained-capabilities-for-taxonomy-terms-in-4-7/&quot;&gt;Fine grained capabilities for taxonomy terms&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/2016/10/29/wp_taxonomy-in-4-7/&quot;&gt;&lt;code&gt;WP_Taxonomy&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/2016/11/02/wp_list_sort-and-wp_list_util-in-4-7/&quot;&gt;&lt;code&gt;wp_list_sort()&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;WP_List_Util&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/2016/11/03/post-type-templates-in-4-7/&quot;&gt;Post type templates&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/2016/11/03/new-post-type-labels-in-4-7/&quot;&gt;New post type labels&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/2016/11/03/attributes-for-resource-hints-in-4-7/&quot;&gt;Attributes for resource hints&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Various bug fixes:&lt;/strong&gt; We’ve made &lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/log/trunk/src?action=stop_on_copy&amp;mode=stop_on_copy&amp;rev=39142&amp;stop_rev=38995&amp;limit=200&amp;verbose=on&amp;sfp_email=&amp;sfph_mail=&quot;&gt;almost 150 changes&lt;/a&gt; in the last week.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;For more of what’s new in version 4.7, &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/news/2016/10/wordpress-4-7-beta-1/&quot;&gt;check out the Beta 1 blog post&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;If you want a more in-depth view of what major changes have made it into 4.7, &lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/tag/4-7/&quot;&gt;check out posts tagged with 4.7 on the main development blog&lt;/a&gt;, or look at a &lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/query?status=closed&amp;resolution=fixed&amp;milestone=4.7&amp;group=component&amp;order=priority&quot;&gt;list of everything&lt;/a&gt; that’s changed. There will be more developer notes to come, so keep an eye out for those as well.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Do you speak a language other than English? &lt;a href=&quot;https://translate.wordpress.org/projects/wp/dev&quot;&gt;Help us translate WordPress into more than 100 languages!&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;If you think you’ve found a bug&lt;/strong&gt;, you can post to the &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/support/forum/alphabeta&quot;&gt;Alpha/Beta area&lt;/a&gt; in the support forums. We’d love to hear from you! If you’re comfortable writing a reproducible bug report, &lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/reports/&quot;&gt;file one on WordPress Trac&lt;/a&gt;, where you can also find &lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/tickets/major&quot;&gt;a list of known bugs&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Happy testing!&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Ya es la hora&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;em&gt; Time for another beta&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
请您帮下忙!&lt;/p&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Fri, 04 Nov 2016 17:39:07 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:15:&quot;Helen Hou-Sandi&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:48;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:85:&quot;WPTavern: A Preview of the Custom CSS Editor Added to the Customizer in WordPress 4.7&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:29:&quot;https://wptavern.com/?p=63481&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:96:&quot;https://wptavern.com/a-preview-of-the-custom-css-editor-added-to-the-customizer-in-wordpress-4-7&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:3295:&quot;&lt;p&gt;WordPress 4.7 is a little more than a &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/about/roadmap/&quot;&gt;month away&lt;/a&gt; and is going to be packed with new features and improvements. In particular, &lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/2016/10/24/customize-update-2016-10-23/&quot;&gt;five feature projects&lt;/a&gt; related to the customizer were approved for merge and will be part of the release. One of the feature projects is the custom &lt;a href=&quot;https://make.wordpress.org/core/2016/10/11/feature-proposal-better-theme-customizations-via-custom-css-with-live-previews/&quot;&gt;CSS editor&lt;/a&gt; that enables users to &lt;a href=&quot;https://wptavern.com/the-days-of-creating-child-themes-for-simple-css-changes-may-soon-be-over&quot;&gt;make CSS changes to a theme&lt;/a&gt; without having to create a &lt;a href=&quot;https://codex.wordpress.org/Child_Themes&quot;&gt;child theme&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;a href=&quot;https://i1.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/11/WP47CustomizerCSSEditor.png?ssl=1&quot;&gt;&lt;img class=&quot;size-full wp-image-63483&quot; src=&quot;https://i1.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/11/WP47CustomizerCSSEditor.png?resize=1025%2C394&amp;ssl=1&quot; alt=&quot;CSS Editor in The WordPress 4.7 Customizer&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;CSS Editor in The WordPress 4.7 Customizer
&lt;p&gt;In WordPress 4.7, there&amp;#8217;s a new section in the customizer labeled Additional CSS. Clicking the label displays a blank pane with a short description of what users can do. Clicking the help icon displays a short explanation of what CSS is with a link to a &lt;a href=&quot;https://codex.wordpress.org/Know_Your_Sources#CSS&quot;&gt;help document&lt;/a&gt; on the Codex. The Additional CSS pane is more like a text area than an editor.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Unlike Jetpack&amp;#8217;s Edit CSS module, the editor in the customizer lacks line numbers, colored text, and other conveniences. However, these are features that are likely to be added in future iterations.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;a href=&quot;https://i1.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/11/JetpacksEditCSSModule.png?ssl=1&quot;&gt;&lt;img class=&quot;size-full wp-image-63484&quot; src=&quot;https://i1.wp.com/wptavern.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/11/JetpacksEditCSSModule.png?resize=601%2C423&amp;ssl=1&quot; alt=&quot;Jetpack's Edit CSS Module&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;Jetpack&amp;#8217;s Edit CSS Module
&lt;p&gt;There are a couple of things to keep in mind before using Additional CSS. First, it does not have revision support enabled. Weston Ruter, WordPress core committer, &lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/ticket/35395#comment:76&quot;&gt;says&lt;/a&gt; revision support is disabled by default and requires a plugin.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Second, changes are theme specific and are not global. Luke Cavanagh &lt;a href=&quot;https://core.trac.wordpress.org/ticket/35395#comment:83&quot;&gt;has inquired&lt;/a&gt; on whether an option will be added in the future to enable global CSS changes which could come in handy for making tweaks for active plugins.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;During testing, I didn&amp;#8217;t encounter any issues with writing or pasting CSS code into the Additional CSS area. I encourage you to download and install &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/news/2016/10/wordpress-4-7-beta-1/&quot;&gt;WordPress 4.7 beta 1&lt;/a&gt; and try it out for yourself and let us know your thoughts. If you think you&amp;#8217;ve encountered a bug while using WordPress 4.7 beta 1, please report it on the &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress.org/support/forum/alphabeta/&quot;&gt;Alpha/Beta section&lt;/a&gt; of the support forums.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;div id=&quot;epoch-width-sniffer&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:7:&quot;pubDate&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:31:&quot;Fri, 04 Nov 2016 08:57:44 +0000&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}s:32:&quot;http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/&quot;;a:1:{s:7:&quot;creator&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;Jeff Chandler&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}}}}i:49;a:6:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:13:&quot;
	
	
	
	
	
	
&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:5:&quot;child&quot;;a:2:{s:0:&quot;&quot;;a:5:{s:5:&quot;title&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:28:&quot;BuddyPress: BuddyPress 2.7.1&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;guid&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:32:&quot;https://buddypress.org/?p=260677&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:4:&quot;link&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:48:&quot;https://buddypress.org/2016/11/buddypress-2-7-1/&quot;;s:7:&quot;attribs&quot;;a:0:{}s:8:&quot;xml_base&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;s:17:&quot;xml_base_explicit&quot;;b:0;s:8:&quot;xml_lang&quot;;s:0:&quot;&quot;;}}s:11:&quot;description&quot;;a:1:{i:0;a:5:{s:4:&quot;data&quot;;s:842:&quot;&lt;p&gt;BuddyPress 2.7.1 is now available. This is a maintenance release and a recommended upgrade for all BuddyPress installations.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;BP 2.7.1 fixes bugs in several components. For more information, see &lt;a href=&quot;https://buddypress.trac.wordpress.org/query?group=status&amp;milestone=2.7.1&quot;&gt;the 2.7.1 milestone&lt;/a&gt; on &lt;a href=&quot;https://buddypress.trac.wordpress.org/&quot;&gt;BuddyPress Trac&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

|2|1|2016-12-08 14:22:14|2016-12-08 14:22:14|This is an example page. It's different from a blog post because it will stay in one place and will show up in your site navigation (in most themes). Most people start with an About page that introduces them to potential site visitors. It might say something like this:

&lt;blockquote&gt;Hi there! I'm a bike messenger by day, aspiring actor by night, and this is my website. I live in Los Angeles, have a great dog named Jack, and I like pi&amp;#241;a coladas. (And gettin' caught in the rain.)&lt;/blockquote&gt;

...or something like this:

&lt;blockquote&gt;The XYZ Doohickey Company was founded in 1971, and has been providing quality doohickeys to the public ever since. Located in Gotham City, XYZ employs over 2,000 people and does all kinds of awesome things for the Gotham community.&lt;/blockquote&gt;
